Hello Everyone Reading This, I would like to first just start off by saying I moved into this neighborhood about 5 years ago and shortly after moving here I really ran into hard times and needed money really quick. I didn`t know anyone around me and other family members were just to far to really help so I just started looking for the closest Pawn Shop near me and found Community which was only around the corner from my house. I looked for stuff I might have that I could pawn to help get the money I so desperately needed and grabbed what few things I had that was worth anything and took them over to Community Pawn and I just can`t express or say just how nice they were to me then and even up until this day almost 5 years latter are the most nicest people I have ever met, especially being in they`re field of business. they`re just really not the kind of people you would think being a pawn shop and of course if you don`t come get you stuff or pay your interest in time they just keep your items to resale for a profit your, well not Community Pawn Shop. They are nothing like that and on the contrary of what most people think about pawn shops all the employees at Community Pawn really have a kind and decent heart and over the past 5 years I have actually went back to them time and time again when times were tuff and just needed a little help to get me by and they have always helped me get through with whatever I needed the best they could with ever I had to pawn, even times when I was late on paying my interest they worked with me so I wouldn`t lose it. I I`m just writing this because I just want everyone taking the time to read this to know that if you are in need of help and really need money for whatever the reason and maybe just a little nervous or scared to pawn your treasured or hard earned items in fear of possibly losing them or anything like that, I can personally tell you there is nothing to worry about when it comes to Community Pawn because as long as you communicate with them and let them know what ever you may be going through in your life, or you`re just short on your payment or just whatever it may be, Community Pawn will never turn there backs or give you the cold shoulder on your pawned items. I can personally promise you they will always do everything in there power to make sure your items are safe and that you will get them back when the time is right for you if you just communicate with them. I can honestly make you this promise because they have personally did it for me a few times over the past 5 years and since that first day I went to them nearly 5 years ago they have now become like very good close friends of mine and we laugh and smile at each other every time I walk through their front door now.
Before ending this review and with hopes by writing it, it help anyone out there that`s thinking if they want to take a chance on pawning any of you personal items or if they are going to be safe or just in fear of possibly losing them or anything like that, please know that Community Pawn is very respectful, trustworthy and honest. They have some of the most awesomest employees I have ever had the pleasure of meeting and doing business with in a time of need. I would like to end this with naming just a few of the awesome people that I have come to know at Community Pawn and that look at and consider like friends,  I say this because a true friend will always be there for you and will always have your back in a time of need and Jaun, Chris and Elmar are just a few of the best people and human beings that I could have ever met when needing help and a little fast cash to get me by. I`ve trusted them with some of my most treasurable, personal and sentimental valuables without fear of losing them. So I`m ending with this, it`s been 5 years and after many many pawns I have not once lost any of my stuff, and there`s actually been a couple times when I surely could have if it were not for Community Pawns understanding and I can promise they will treat you and any one else the same exact way. Thanks Community Pawn.< /review>

All we wanted was a decent office chair to replace the defective chair we purchased here a month ago.  They would not attempt to fix it, as over 30 days had passed, so we decided to simply purchase a new one.

Here is what I have found after two months.

Antiquated features and appliances with quirky defects: refrigerator freezes everything even at the minimal setting, garbage disposal has already failed after two weeks into contract, overhead kitchen vent only works at the lowest setting, stove top burners operate at wildly varying heats, the air conditioner inside the apartment ceiling sounds a lot like a lawnmower engine, air pollutants from ventilation have plagued me with off/on illness for over six weeks and dumps a strange odor into the dwelling, very weak water pressure from both faucets,  the community laundry facility is only open during business hours and gets extremely hot and crowded as well as disgustingly odorous since multiple washers don't drain properly, management will have your vehicle towed without warning because they don't make the effort to maintain a proper tenant vehicle registry, lawn care personnel blow pine needles and debris through my door threshold when clearing the walkways, sliding closet doors are old/shoddy and all of the other pantry/closet doors are assembled with basic spring latches and no bolt catch so they are always slightly open...I could obviously continue but will conclude by adding that this is supposedly a "renovated" unit.

I have confirmed this pattern with a former tenant.

<Name>Amber Strum</Name><Date>1487232441232< /Date><rating>4< /rating>< Review>
Love the food here most of the time. Our last trip the tri tip fries had a bit too much dressing on them which caused the fries to be soggy at the bottom.
The staff is friendly. Seems like the seating is a little out of sorts and they're still trying to decide if it's a formal dining restaurant or casual. Lunch hours you order at the register and then seat yourself with a number. Evening, you're seated by a waitress.
The menu you're given in the evening could use some descriptions for some of the items.
Overall I'm looking forward to seeing improvements as time passes and love the food!< /Review>

Value: 7 was a bit pricey than most juice bars in area but you get what you pay for I suppose.
style/vibe: when I came in I was immediately greeted by a  very polite gentlemen.

Location 8.5 located right off winchester was barely any parking due to trader Joe's sharing same parking lot.

Cleanliness: 10 every table and counter top was clean floors were clean and  I  personally witnessed employees routinely washing there hands before they touched anything which is always a plus.

Final opinion great tasting juice bar definitely top 2  in Temecula in my opinion.  was a bit pricey I paid about 8 bucks for a bowl but ingredients are all natural so I know exactly what is in my bowl.

All in All: Yes I would recommend this place if you have the time and money to get an great tasting smoothie or bowl.  -LawrenceK< /Review>

<text>Ok, not sure where to start, I got mixed feelings.

I was here almost 3 years ago on a Sunday morning for the very first time, and yes, I loved it, reason why I was back today.

Since then, I have been back to Paso about 4-5 times and I was not able to get a reservation again because L'Aventure was always sold out which is great, I guess people love it.

I decided to drive into town today from LA to treat some friends with a great wine experience. I gave L'Aventure a call in the morning to see if they could accommodate us even though they were booked for the day online. Nicole graciously was able to find a spot for us towards the end of the day. I give them credit for that, maybe because I mentioned I was there before, that I love the scenery and was planning on joining the wine club, I don't know if that was the ultimate reason but yes, they got me in. Thank you for that Nicole!

We showed up right on the dot, sat and the whole flight was provided in a nice woody tray. She recited what the wines were, I mean the names of the wines; no further explanation about the wines, the story behind L'Adventure and how they differentiate from their neighbors. She didn't offer nor make any interest about selling the wine club to me, even thought I had volunteered earlier in my call I was interested on joining the club.

To be honest, it was like from day to night, comparing my first experience to this one, even the wines tasted like whatever today.

My recommendation to Stephan(L'Adventure's owner), please send your tasting room employees to your "Favorite Neighbor"(Booker), like the way they refer to L'Adventure, so your employees could learn customer service etiquete from them.

Ok, long story short, after we finished the tasting, I went inside, pulled my credit card out, paid and more importantly I was not asked if was interested on buying anything or if I wanted to revisit any wine, etc.

My recommendation to other wine lovers who are coming down to Paso, stay away and certainly visit other wineries such as Alta Colima, Law or Booker. You will appreciate my recommendation.<//text><username>Frank Garcia</username>< UserId.>

<UserId.>108107885722943817698</UserId.>< review>
The wife and I were having an anniversary getaway in Santa Barbara and while visiting Jamie Slone we were told that we needed to visit L'aventure. The tasting room is appointment only so I made an appointment for the next day.

L'aventure is a bit out of the way, you even travel on a dirt road for part of the way. But when you finally arrive at the wooden gate and drive up to the tasting room you'll swear you hear angels singing softly.

The facility is nestled between 2 vine covered hills in an idyllic setting. Just stop and take a look around before you begin your tasting. This can't help but put you in the right frame of mind. The tasting room is a modern marvel of sleek concrete and glass.

We were about 10 minutes late for our appointment as the drive from Santa Barbara took a little longer than expected but we were greeted immediately and got taken care of by Leanne. She was a fountain of knowledge about  L'aventure and wines in general. We had a great time getting to know her and the winery. All of the wines we tasted were excellent. We especially liked the Cote de Cote and the Estate Cuvee, smooth mouth feel with big, velvety fruit. For years I've said that my limit for a bottle of wine was $50. The Cote de Cote and Cuvee were both $100 and I bought a bottle of each. That's how good they were.

Who would have thought that little old Paso Robles would become a hotbed of wine production but it certainly has.  If it weren't for recommendation of Jamie and Kim at Jamie Slone we never would have found about this diamond in Paso.

Why are you still reading this review? Call L'aventure and make an appointment of your own. You won't regret it.<//review>

< Review>
Great food, great service. Fast service too considering I went during the dinner rush hour. It seems a bit pricey at first but the food is definitely worth it! Tons of options and a few unique burgers too. I believe they also have vegetarian burgers as well which is a nice inclusion to have for vegetarian people.
Outdoor dining during Covid is nice although it can feel a little cramped but definitely one of the better restaurants to go to during this time. They have a firm grip on the situation and have barriers between tables as well which I haven't seen in many other places.<//Review>

< text>
Prepare to drop $25 for a half pound burger and onion rings, $7 for a milkshake. If you can get past that, prepare for some truly amazing food! This time I  had a Caribbean burger, filled with grilled jerk rubbed veggies, and a well done (my choice) flame grilled patty. The basket of huge, perfectly cooked onion rings topped with melted parmesan cheese would have been  enough without the burger.  Still, looked forward to having half the burger for dinner. This is not a place to go all the time, but you owe it to yourself to see how well a burger can be made.<//text>

<user>105327081310360353311<//user>< username>
Richie Zeng</username>
<date>1582609227977<//date><rate>5</rate><review>This is my go-to place whenever we have people visiting Berkeley and want to get a large group together to eat. They always seem to have just enough space to fit our group, ranging anywhere from 4-10.

They have a great selection of burgers, all of them great. My personal favorites are Maui Waui, Baja, and Hickory.

The fries are delicious and come in huge portions. We usually get a full size serving of fries to split. The only fries I wouldn't recommend are the truffle fries. You can smell the truffle oil, but it doesn't really impact the taste, especially if you're going to be dipping them in ketchup.

Really generous portions. Expect to be stuffed by the time you're through with your burger and fries. If you get a shake in on top of that...well, good luck. I still feel full by the time I should be eating my next meal.</review>< pics>

< userid>
101229155541175109091<//userid>
< user_name>
Lesther Papa</user_name>
< time>
1568685622250< /time>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
We got to the restaurant and it's pretty amazing! There is a great patio area and in the restaurant is cozy with wood furniture and a fireplace. There isn't a lot of street parking in this area but there is a Safeway right across the street.

The servers were really attentive to our needs and were really quick at taking our order. Food came out super quick. We ordered curly fries, the Big Barney, and the Voodoo Burger. The fries were on our table in less than 10 minutes and the our burgers were there in another 10 minutes. The fries were super fresh and hot. The ranch they have for it seems homemade and pairs well with the fries. Our burgers were hot and juicy. I would have liked my bun to be toasted and the pattie to be more heavily seasoned but it was still an excellent burger and nothing a salt shaker and pepper grinder could not fix (they were already there on the table along with ketchup, mustard, Dijon, and Tabasco).

Overall we had an excellent experience and I'm sure we'll be back soon.</Review>

Now I know why everytime I go on about a giant hamburger someone asks me if I've been to Barney's ‚Äî these are burgers of epic proportions! I had the Morrocan burger, which was spicy, and topped with provolone and 1000 Island dressing (my prime condiment weakness). Barney's gets extra points for having gluten-free buns, and knowing which of their many fry options are *actually* gluten-free. Grass-fed beef, turkey, salmon, and garden (also Beyond) burgers make it possible to kick back for burger time with anyone that isn't a Breatherarian. The salads look equally as amazing, but I never made it that far and I had enough lettuce on my burger to satisfy the customary vegetable requirement.</text>

<Text>This was one of the best burgers I've ever eaten. I got the Gastropub Burger, a 1/2 lb of Certified Angus Beef cooked medium, served on a pretzel bun and topped with provolone, bacon (perfectly cooked and flavored), a fried egg, and blackened potato chips. It was as red, juicy, and flavorful as you could wish. The steak fries were the Platonic ideal of steak fries. < Text>
Quickie:
+ Lived in North Berkeley for 3 years during college and only one block away from the Gourmet Ghetto - so to say I frequented Barney's is an understatement.
+ Friggin' amazing burgers

---

Food:
What can I say? The burgers are delicious as are their fries (both steak cut and sweet potato). It's hard to narrow down but I think the French burger is my favorite (Crumbled Bleu cheese and bacon, yum). But in the number of times I've been there, I've probably tried over half the menu and my friends accounted for the rest. Always spectacular, very different combinations - just an all-around nice burger joint.

Overall:
They do take-out. as well, so if you have a midterm to cram for back at home, just call in and pick up in 15. All in all, Barney's is a great alternative to a greasy fast food burger - they do gourmet on a broke college kid's budget.</Text>
